ACTOR BlueBeachPig : PigCop
{
	DropItem "RandomBeachPigDrop", 256, 1
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			DN53 A 0
			DN53 A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
			DN53 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
			DN53 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
		Spawn2:
			DN53 A 1 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			DN53 A 3 A_Chase
			DN53 A 3 A_Chase
			DN53 B 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			DN53 B 3 A_Chase
			DN53 C 3 A_Chase
			DN53 C 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			DN53 D 3 A_Chase
			DN53 D 3 A_Chase
			Loop
		Missile:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump (64, "ProneShot")
			Goto StandShot
		StandShot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
			DN53 EE 5 A_FaceTarget
			DN53 E 3
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/mossberg", CHAN_WEAPON)
			TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PigCopBullet",32,0,random(-12,12),8,random(-12,12))
			DN53 F 15 Bright
			DN53 G 7 A_PlaySound("duke/mosspump2", 5)
			DN53 EE 5 A_FaceTarget
			DN53 E 7 
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/mossberg", CHAN_WEAPON)
			TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PigCopBullet",32,0,random(-12,12),8,random(-12,12))
			DN53 F 16 Bright
			DN53 G 7 A_PlaySound("duke/mosspump2", 5)
			DN53 E 9 A_CPosRefire
			Goto See
		ProneShot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
			DN53 H 11 A_FaceTarget
			DN53 IIIIII 5 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PigProneBullet",32,0,random(-12,12),8,random(-12,12))
			DN53 J 18 Bright A_PlaySound("duke/mossberg", CHAN_WEAPON)
			DN53 I 17 A_PlaySound("duke/mosspump2", 5)
			TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PigProneBullet",32,0,random(-12,12),8,random(-12,12))
			DN53 J 16 Bright A_PlaySound("duke/mossberg", CHAN_WEAPON)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/mosspump2", 5)
			TNT1 A 0 A_CPosRefire
			Goto See
		Pain:

			DN53 K 16 A_Pain
			Goto See
		Pain.MarathonStun:

			TNT1 A -1
			stop
		Ice:
		Death.HexenIce:
		Death.WTMeleeIce:
		Death.WTRangedIce:
		Death.Ice:

			DN53 PONMLK 5
			Goto See
		Death.CalebNapalm:

	}
}

Actor BlueBeachPigCorpse
{
	Health 20
	Height 8
	Radius 16
	Mass 5000
	BloodType "DukeBlood"
	+ISMONSTER
	-COUNTKILL
	-SHOOTABLE
	+VULNERABLE
	-SOLID
	+NOTARGET
	-FRIENDLY
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			DN53 P 4
			Loop
		Death:
			TNT1 A 0 A_RemoveMaster
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)

			TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnDebris("DukeJibs6")
			TNT1 A 5 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib")
			Stop
		Death.RottDisintegrate:
			"####" "#" 0 A_RemoveMaster
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Stop

			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItem("RGodModeDeathSmall")

actor BlueBeachPig_Shrink : BlueBeachPig
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE

	+NODAMAGE

	MaxDropOffHeight 0

	Height 16

	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:

			DN53 K 10

			DN53 A 1 A_Look
			Loop
		See:

			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)

			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)

ACTOR RedBeachPig : PigCop
{
	DropItem "RandomBeachPigDrop", 256, 1
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			DN54 A 0
			DN54 A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
			DN54 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
			DN54 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
		Spawn2:
			DN54 A 1 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			DN54 A 3 A_Chase
			DN54 A 3 A_Chase
			DN54 B 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			DN54 B 3 A_Chase
			DN54 C 3 A_Chase
			DN54 C 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			DN54 D 3 A_Chase
			DN54 D 3 A_Chase
			Loop
		Missile:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump (64, "ProneShot")
			Goto StandShot
		StandShot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
			DN54 EE 5 A_FaceTarget
			DN54 E 3
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/mossberg", CHAN_WEAPON)
			TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PigCopBullet",32,0,random(-12,12),8,random(-12,12))
			DN54 F 15 Bright
			DN54 G 7 A_PlaySound("duke/mosspump2", 5)
			DN54 EE 5 A_FaceTarget
			DN54 E 7 
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/mossberg", CHAN_WEAPON)
			TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PigCopBullet",32,0,random(-12,12),8,random(-12,12))
			DN54 F 16 Bright
			DN54 G 7 A_PlaySound("duke/mosspump2", 5)
			DN54 E 9 A_CPosRefire
			Goto See
		ProneShot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
			DN54 H 11 A_FaceTarget
			DN54 IIIIII 5 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PigProneBullet",32,0,random(-12,12),8,random(-12,12))
			DN54 J 18 Bright A_PlaySound("duke/mossberg", CHAN_WEAPON)
			DN54 I 17 A_PlaySound("duke/mosspump2", 5)
			TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PigProneBullet",32,0,random(-12,12),8,random(-12,12))

actor RedBeachPig_Shrink : RedBeachPig
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			DN54 K 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			DN54 A 1 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN54 A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN54 A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN54 B 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN54 B 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN54 C 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN54 C 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN54 D 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN54 D 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			DN55 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
			DN55 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
		Spawn2:
			DN55 A 1 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			DN55 A 3 A_Chase
			DN55 A 3 A_Chase

		Missile:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump (64, "ProneShot")
			Goto StandShot
		StandShot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
			DN55 EE 5 A_FaceTarget
			DN55 E 3
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/mossberg", CHAN_WEAPON)
			TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PigCopBullet",32,0,random(-12,12),8,random(-12,12))

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
			loop
		ExpanderPop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
		Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
			DN55 A 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
		ExpanderLoopCoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
			loop
		ExpanderPopCoop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
	}
}

actor GreenBeachPig_Shrink : GreenBeachPig
{

	+NOTRIGGER

		See:

			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:

ACTOR GrayBeachPig : PigCop
{
	DropItem "RandomBeachPigDrop", 256, 1
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			DN56 A 0
			DN56 A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
			DN56 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
			DN56 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
		Spawn2:
			DN56 A 1 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			DN56 A 3 A_Chase
			DN56 A 3 A_Chase
			DN56 B 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			DN56 B 3 A_Chase
			DN56 C 3 A_Chase
			DN56 C 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			DN56 D 3 A_Chase
			DN56 D 3 A_Chase
			Loop
		Missile:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump (64, "ProneShot")
			Goto StandShot
		StandShot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
			DN56 EE 5 A_FaceTarget
			DN56 E 3
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/mossberg", CHAN_WEAPON)
			TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PigCopBullet",32,0,random(-12,12),8,random(-12,12))
			DN56 F 15 Bright
			DN56 G 7 A_PlaySound("duke/mosspump2", 5)
			DN56 EE 5 A_FaceTarget
			DN56 E 7 
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/mossberg", CHAN_WEAPON)
			TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PigCopBullet",32,0,random(-12,12),8,random(-12,12))
			DN56 F 16 Bright
			DN56 G 7 A_PlaySound("duke/mosspump2", 5)
			DN56 E 9 A_CPosRefire
			Goto See
		ProneShot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
			DN56 H 11 A_FaceTarget
			DN56 IIIIII 5 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PigProneBullet",32,0,random(-12,12),8,random(-12,12))
			DN56 J 18 Bright A_PlaySound("duke/mossberg", CHAN_WEAPON)
			DN56 I 17 A_PlaySound("duke/mosspump2", 5)
			TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PigProneBullet",32,0,random(-12,12),8,random(-12,12))
			DN56 J 16 Bright A_PlaySound("duke/mossberg", CHAN_WEAPON)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/mosspump2", 5)
			TNT1 A 0 A_CPosRefire
			Goto See
		Pain:
			DN56 K 3
			DN56 K 3 A_Pain
			Goto See
		Pain.MightyBoot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
			DN56 K 2 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(14)
			DN56 K 16 A_Pain
			Goto See

		See:

		Missile:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump (64, "ProneShot")
			Goto StandShot

			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
			DN57 EE 5 A_FaceTarget
			DN57 E 3
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/mossberg", CHAN_WEAPON)

			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)

			Stop
		Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
			DN57 A 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)

			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)

		ExpanderPopCoop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
	}

actor DarkGrayBeachPig_Shrink : DarkGrayBeachPig
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			DN57 K 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			DN57 A 1 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN57 A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN57 A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN57 B 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN57 B 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN57 C 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN57 C 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)

			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)

			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DarkGrayBeachPig", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_DamageChildren(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker",2))
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish

ACTOR BrownBeachPig : PigCop
{
	DropItem "RandomBeachPigDrop", 256, 1
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			DN59 A 0
			DN59 A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
			DN59 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
			DN59 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
		Spawn2:
			DN59 A 1 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			DN59 A 3 A_Chase
			DN59 A 3 A_Chase
			DN59 B 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			DN59 B 3 A_Chase
			DN59 C 3 A_Chase
			DN59 C 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			DN59 D 3 A_Chase
			DN59 D 3 A_Chase
			Loop
		Missile:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump (64, "ProneShot")
			Goto StandShot
		StandShot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
			DN59 EE 5 A_FaceTarget
			DN59 E 3
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/mossberg", CHAN_WEAPON)
			TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PigCopBullet",32,0,random(-12,12),8,random(-12,12))
			DN59 F 15 Bright
			DN59 G 7 A_PlaySound("duke/mosspump2", 5)
			DN59 EE 5 A_FaceTarget
			DN59 E 7 
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/mossberg", CHAN_WEAPON)
			TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PigCopBullet",32,0,random(-12,12),8,random(-12,12))
			DN59 F 16 Bright
			DN59 G 7 A_PlaySound("duke/mosspump2", 5)
			DN59 E 9 A_CPosRefire
			Goto See
		ProneShot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
			DN59 H 11 A_FaceTarget

actor BrownBeachPig_Shrink : BrownBeachPig
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			DN59 K 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			DN59 A 1 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN59 A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN59 A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN59 B 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)

{

	{
		Spawn:
			DN60 A 0

			DN60 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
			DN60 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
		Spawn2:
			DN60 A 1 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			DN60 A 3 A_Chase
			DN60 A 3 A_Chase
			DN60 B 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			DN60 B 3 A_Chase

			DN60 C 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			DN60 D 3 A_Chase
			DN60 D 3 A_Chase
			Loop
		Missile:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump (64, "ProneShot")
			Goto StandShot
		StandShot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
			DN60 EE 5 A_FaceTarget
			DN60 E 3
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/mossberg", CHAN_WEAPON)
			TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("PigCopBullet",32,0,random(-12,12),8,random(-12,12))
			DN60 F 15 Bright
			DN60 G 7 A_PlaySound("duke/mosspump2", 5)

			DN60 E 7 
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/mossberg", CHAN_WEAPON)

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("YellowBeachPig_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("YellowBeachPig_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("YellowBeachPig_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("YellowBeachPig_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 2
			TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Death.ExpanderDMG:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
			DN60 A 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoop
		ExpanderLoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
			loop
		ExpanderPop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
		Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
			DN60 A 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
		ExpanderLoopCoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
			loop
		ExpanderPopCoop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
	}

actor YellowBeachPig_Shrink : YellowBeachPig
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			DN60 K 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			DN60 A 1 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN60 A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN60 A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN60 B 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN60 B 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN60 C 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN60 C 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN60 D 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN60 D 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("YellowBeachPig", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_DamageChildren(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker",2))
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}
}

ACTOR DarkGreenBeachPig : PigCop
{
	DropItem "RandomBeachPigDrop", 256, 1
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			DN61 A 0
			DN61 A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
			DN61 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
			DN61 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
		Spawn2:
			DN61 A 1 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			DN61 A 3 A_Chase

			"####" "#" 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.4,0)
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)
			"####" "#" 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.3,0)
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)
			"####" "#" 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.2,0)
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)
			"####" "#" 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,0)
			stop
		Disintegrate:
			"####" "#" 0 A_RemoveMaster
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("SHOOTABLE",FALSE)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Stop
			"####" "#" 3 A_SpawnItem("DisintEffectSmall",0,10)
			"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.9,0)
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)

			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)
			"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.7,0)
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)
			"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.6,0)
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)
			"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.5,0)
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)
			"####" "#" 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.4,0)
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)
			"####" "#" 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.3,0)
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)
			"####" "#" 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.2,0)
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)
			"####" "#" 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,0)
			stop
		Death.Nuke:
			"####" "#" 0 A_RemoveMaster
			"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("SHOOTABLE",FALSE)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItem("WTNukeDeathSmall")
			"####" "#################" 3 A_Fadeout(0.05)
			stop
		Death.DukeIce:
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemyfreeze")
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("FreezethrowerWeakness")
		Ice:
		Death.HexenIce:
		Death.WTMeleeIce:
		Death.WTRangedIce:
		Death.Ice:
			"####" "#" 0 A_RemoveMaster
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)

			"####" "#" 70 A_UnsetSolid
			"####" "#" 0 A_IceGuyDie
			"####" "#" 1 A_IceGuyDie
			TNT1 A 0
			stop
	}

actor DarkGreenBeachPig_Shrink : DarkGreenBeachPig
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			DN61 K 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			DN61 A 1 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN61 A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN61 A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN61 B 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN61 B 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN61 C 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN61 C 3 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN61 D 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			DN61 D 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DarkGreenBeachPig", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_DamageChildren(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker",2))
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}
}
